## 1. EXECUTIVE SUMMARY

**INFINITY XOS** is an autonomous AI operating system designed to function as a self-evolving, self-healing intelligence platform. The system combines multiple AI agents, real-time data processing, predictive analytics, and autonomous execution capabilities into a unified ecosystem.

### Core Philosophy

> "Intelligence Redefined" â€” A system that doesn't just respond to commands but anticipates needs, learns from patterns, and executes autonomously while maintaining human oversight.

### Key Capabilities

| Capability | Description |
|------------|-------------|
| **Autonomous Agents** | Self-directed AI workers that execute tasks 24/7 |
| **Vision Cortex** | Real-time market analysis and pattern recognition |
| **Predictive Engine** | ML-powered forecasting across multiple domains |
| **Memory System** | Persistent context and learning across sessions |
| **Auto Builder** | Autonomous code generation and deployment |
| **Template System** | Reusable workflows for rapid deployment |

### 4.2 Page Details

| Page | Purpose | Key Components |
|------|---------|----------------|
| **Dashboard** | Central command center | System status, quick actions, recent activity, agent overview |
| **Vision Cortex** | Real-time market intelligence | Live charts, heatmaps, alerts, pattern detection |
| **Agent Builder** | Create custom AI agents | Visual workflow builder, prompt editor, test sandbox |
| **Quantum X** | Predictive analytics | Forecasting models, scenario simulator, risk analysis |
| **Templates** | Reusable workflows | Template library, import/export, customization |
| **Memory** | Context management | Memory viewer, knowledge base, training data |

### 6.2 Industry-Specific Pipelines

| Industry | Data Sources | Key Metrics | Automation |
|----------|--------------|-------------|------------|
| **Real Estate (Florida)** | County records, MLS, foreclosure lists | Equity %, Days on market, Price/sqft | Property alerts, CMA generation |
| **Platinum Funding** | Business registrations, Revenue data | Revenue, Years in business, Credit signals | Pre-qualification, Doc requests |
| **Crypto/DeFi** | Chain data, Wallet analytics | TVL, Volume, Holder distribution | Opportunity alerts, Risk scoring |
| **Stocks/Options** | Market feeds, SEC filings | P/E, Volume, Insider activity | Trade signals, Portfolio rebalance |

---

### 9.2 Auto Builder Capabilities

| Capability | Description | Output |
|------------|-------------|--------|
| **Full Stack App** | Complete web application from description | React + Node + DB |
| **API Endpoint** | Single API with documentation | Express/FastAPI route |
| **Database Schema** | Data model from requirements | SQL/NoSQL schema |
| **UI Component** | React component from design | TSX + Tailwind |
| **Integration** | Connect two systems | Webhook/API bridge |
| **Automation** | Workflow from description | Cloud Function |

---


### 12.2 Security Layers

| Layer | Implementation | Purpose |
|-------|----------------|---------|
| **Transport** | HTTPS/TLS | Encrypt data in transit |
| **Authentication** | Manus OAuth + JWT | Verify user identity |
| **Authorization** | Role-based (admin/user) | Control access |
| **API Security** | Rate limiting, CORS | Prevent abuse |
| **Data Security** | Encryption at rest | Protect stored data |
| **Secret Management** | Environment variables | Secure credentials |

---

## 5.2 Vision Cortex Data Flow

```
STEP 1: DATA INGESTION (Every 15 seconds)
â”œâ”€â”€ Market APIs â†’ Finnhub, Alpha Vantage, CoinGecko
â”œâ”€â”€ Social APIs â†’ Twitter/X, Reddit, Discord
â”œâ”€â”€ News APIs â†’ NewsAPI, Google News
â””â”€â”€ Alternative Data â†’ Weather, Satellite, IoT

STEP 2: PREPROCESSING
â”œâ”€â”€ Normalize all data to common schema
â”œâ”€â”€ Apply time-series alignment
â”œâ”€â”€ Remove noise and outliers
â””â”€â”€ Cache in Redis for fast access

STEP 3: FEATURE EXTRACTION
â”œâ”€â”€ Technical indicators (RSI, MACD, Bollinger)
â”œâ”€â”€ Sentiment scores (-1 to +1)
â”œâ”€â”€ Volume anomalies
â”œâ”€â”€ Cross-asset correlations
â””â”€â”€ Temporal patterns

STEP 4: PREDICTION GENERATION
â”œâ”€â”€ Short-term (1-24 hours)
â”œâ”€â”€ Medium-term (1-7 days)
â”œâ”€â”€ Long-term (1-4 weeks)
â””â”€â”€ Each with confidence interval

STEP 5: STRATEGY SYNTHESIS
â”œâ”€â”€ Entry/Exit points
â”œâ”€â”€ Position sizing
â”œâ”€â”€ Risk parameters
â”œâ”€â”€ Stop-loss levels
â””â”€â”€ Take-profit targets

STEP 6: OUTPUT DELIVERY
â”œâ”€â”€ Dashboard real-time update
â”œâ”€â”€ Push notifications (critical alerts)
â”œâ”€â”€ Email digest (daily summary)
â”œâ”€â”€ API webhook (for auto-trading)
â””â”€â”€ Voice briefing (Aura)
```

## 5.3 Vision Cortex API Endpoints

```typescript
// Cloud Run: vision-cortex-service

// Get real-time market analysis
GET /api/v1/vision/analyze
Query: { asset: "BTC", timeframe: "1h" }
Response: {
  prediction: { direction: "bullish", confidence: 78.5 },
  signals: [...],
  risk_score: 42,
  suggested_action: "HOLD"
}

// Get multi-asset correlation matrix
GET /api/v1/vision/correlations
Response: {
  matrix: [[1.0, 0.85, -0.32], ...],
  assets: ["BTC", "ETH", "SPY"],
  updated_at: "2026-01-07T..."
}

// Get anomaly alerts
GET /api/v1/vision/anomalies
Response: {
  anomalies: [
    { asset: "ETH", type: "volume_spike", severity: "high", timestamp: "..." }
  ]
}

// Generate strategy
POST /api/v1/vision/strategy
Body: { portfolio: [...], risk_tolerance: "moderate", horizon: "7d" }
Response: {
  strategy: {
    allocations: [...],
    rebalance_triggers: [...],
    expected_return: 4.2,
    max_drawdown: 8.5
  }
}
```

## 6.3 Auto Builder Code Generation Flow

```typescript
// Step 1: Parse user intent
const intent = await parseIntent(userPrompt);
// { type: "crud_app", entities: ["lead"], features: ["map", "email"] }

// Step 2: Generate database schema
const schema = await generateSchema(intent.entities);
// CREATE TABLE leads (id, name, email, property_address, status, created_at)

// Step 3: Generate API routes
const routes = await generateRoutes(schema);
// GET /api/leads, POST /api/leads, PUT /api/leads/:id, DELETE /api/leads/:id

// Step 4: Generate frontend components
const components = await generateComponents(intent.features);
// LeadTable.tsx, LeadForm.tsx, LeadMap.tsx, LeadEmailer.tsx

// Step 5: Generate pages
const pages = await generatePages(components);
// /leads, /leads/new, /leads/:id, /leads/map

// Step 6: Wire everything together
const app = await assembleApp({ schema, routes, components, pages });

// Step 7: Deploy
const url = await deployToCloudRun(app);
```

---

## 7.2 Manus MCP Tool Usage

```bash
# Gmail MCP - Send notifications
manus-mcp-cli tool call send_email --server gmail --input '{
  "to": "user@example.com",
  "subject": "New Lead Alert",
  "body": "A new distressed property lead has been found..."
}'

# Calendar MCP - Schedule tasks
manus-mcp-cli tool call create_event --server google-calendar --input '{
  "summary": "Review Vision Cortex Predictions",
  "start": "2026-01-08T09:00:00",
  "end": "2026-01-08T10:00:00"
}'

# Stripe MCP - Process payments
manus-mcp-cli tool call create_payment_intent --server stripe --input '{
  "amount": 9900,
  "currency": "usd",
  "customer": "cus_xxx"
}'

# Playwright MCP - Browser automation
manus-mcp-cli tool call browser_navigate --server playwright --input '{
  "url": "https://target-site.com/listings"
}'
```

# PART 9: DATABASE SCHEMA

## 9.1 Core Tables

```sql
-- Users (Manus OAuth)
CREATE TABLE users (
  id VARCHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
  open_id VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
  name VARCHAR(255),
  email VARCHAR(255),
  avatar_url TEXT,
  role ENUM('user', 'admin') DEFAULT 'user',
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Agent Memory
CREATE TABLE agent_memory (
  id VARCHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
  user_id VARCHAR(36) REFERENCES users(id),
  agent_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  memory_type ENUM('short_term', 'long_term', 'episodic', 'semantic'),
  content JSON NOT NULL,
  embedding VECTOR(1536),
  importance_score FLOAT DEFAULT 0.5,
  access_count INT DEFAULT 0,
  last_accessed TIMESTAMP,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  expires_at TIMESTAMP
);

-- Conversations
CREATE TABLE conversations (
  id VARCHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
  user_id VARCHAR(36) REFERENCES users(id),
  title VARCHAR(255),
  agent_type VARCHAR(50),
  message_count INT DEFAULT 0,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Messages
CREATE TABLE messages (
  id VARCHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
  conversation_id VARCHAR(36) REFERENCES conversations(id),
  role ENUM('user', 'assistant', 'system'),
  content TEXT NOT NULL,
  tokens_used INT,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Predictions (Vision Cortex)
CREATE TABLE predictions (
  id VARCHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
  user_id VARCHAR(36) REFERENCES users(id),
  asset VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
  timeframe VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
  prediction_type ENUM('price', 'trend', 'volatility'),
  predicted_value DECIMAL(20, 8),
  confidence FLOAT,
  actual_value DECIMAL(20, 8),
  accuracy FLOAT,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  resolved_at TIMESTAMP
);

-- Leads (Scraper Output)
CREATE TABLE leads (
  id VARCHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
  source VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  lead_type ENUM('distressed_property', 'business_funding', 'other'),
  score INT DEFAULT 0,
  status ENUM('new', 'contacted', 'qualified', 'converted', 'dead') DEFAULT 'new',
  data JSON NOT NULL,
  contact_info JSON,
  notes TEXT,
  assigned_to VARCHAR(36) REFERENCES users(id),
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Scraper Runs
CREATE TABLE scraper_runs (
  id VARCHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
  scraper_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  status ENUM('running', 'completed', 'failed'),
  records_found INT DEFAULT 0,
  records_new INT DEFAULT 0,
  error_message TEXT,
  started_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  completed_at TIMESTAMP
);

-- Generated Apps (Auto Builder)
CREATE TABLE generated_apps (
  id VARCHAR(36) PRIMARY KEY,
  user_id VARCHAR(36) REFERENCES users(id),
  name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  description TEXT,
  template VARCHAR(50),
  config JSON,
  deployment_url TEXT,
  status ENUM('generating', 'deployed', 'failed'),
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);
```

# PART 10: API REFERENCE

## 10.1 tRPC Procedures

```typescript
// Authentication
auth.me.useQuery()                    // Get current user
auth.logout.useMutation()             // Logout

// Vision Cortex
vision.analyze.useQuery({ asset, timeframe })
vision.predict.useMutation({ asset, horizon })
vision.getHistory.useQuery({ asset, limit })
vision.getAlerts.useQuery()

// Agent Memory
memory.store.useMutation({ content, type })
memory.search.useQuery({ query, limit })
memory.getContext.useQuery({ conversationId })

// Conversations
conversations.list.useQuery()
conversations.create.useMutation({ title, agentType })
conversations.delete.useMutation({ id })

// Messages
messages.list.useQuery({ conversationId })
messages.send.useMutation({ conversationId, content })
messages.stream.useSubscription({ conversationId })

// Leads
leads.list.useQuery({ type, status, limit })
leads.get.useQuery({ id })
leads.update.useMutation({ id, status, notes })
leads.export.useMutation({ format })

// Auto Builder
builder.generate.useMutation({ prompt })
builder.getStatus.useQuery({ appId })
builder.deploy.useMutation({ appId })
builder.list.useQuery()

// Admin
admin.users.list.useQuery()
admin.users.update.useMutation({ id, role })
admin.scrapers.list.useQuery()
admin.scrapers.run.useMutation({ name })
admin.scrapers.getStats.useQuery()
```
